#AI_AGGRESSION_MORE

ai_aggression_more_status_GER = { reversed = yes allowed = { tag = GER OR = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_aggression_status option = AI_AGGRESSION_MORE } has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG } } enable_reverse = { GER = { is_subject = no num_divisions > 0 } } enable = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_aggression_status option = AI_AGGRESSION_MORE } has_global_flag = AI_AGGRESSION_MORE_FLAG NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } is_neighbor_of = GER } target_array = GER.neighbors abort_when_not_enabled = yes ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "GER" value = 75 } ai_strategy = { type = conquer id = "GER" value = 75 } ai_strategy = { type = declare_war id = "GER" value = 75 }	ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "GER" value = 75 } }

#AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_25

ai_division_limiter_25 = {
	allowed = {
		has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_limiter_status option = AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_25 }
	}
	enable = {
		has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_limiter_status option = AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_25 }
		num_divisions > 25
		is_major = no
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = cavalry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = garrison			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = paratroopers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = mountaineers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = marines			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armor			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = light_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = heavy_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = medium_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = modern_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = infantry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armored_car		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = artillery		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = rocket			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized_rocket	value = -9999 }
}

#AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_DYNAMIC

ai_division_limiter_dynamic = {
	allowed = {
		has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_limiter_status option = AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_DYNAMIC }
	}
	enable = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = GER_ai_behavior
								option = DEFAULT
							}
						}	
					}
					has_country_flag = GER_AI_RANDOM_FASCIST
					has_global_flag = NW_GER_AI_FASCIST
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_ai_behavior
						option = FASCIST
					}
				}
			}
			date > 1940.1.1
		}
# ПОЧИНИТЬ ПОТОМ		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
				OR = {
#					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
#						OR = {
#							not = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
#							has_game_rule = {
#								rule = JAP_ai_behavior
#								option = DEFAULT
#							}
#						}
#					}
#					has_game_rule = {
#						rule = JAP_ai_behavior
#						option = FASCIST
#					}
					has_country_flag = JAP_AI_RANDOM_FASCIST
				}
			}
			date > 1940.1.1
		}
		has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_limiter_status option = AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_DYNAMIC }
		check_variable = { num_divisions > ai_upper_limit }
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = cavalry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = garrison			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = paratroopers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = mountaineers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = marines			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armor			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = light_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = heavy_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = medium_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = modern_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = infantry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armored_car		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = artillery		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = rocket			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized_rocket	value = -9999 }
}

ai_division_limiter_american_full_stop = {
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			tag = JAM
			tag = COS
			tag = PAN
			tag = SUR
			tag = VEN
			tag = COL
			tag = ECU
			tag = KEC
			tag = PAR
			tag = PRU
			tag = PAU
			tag = JUL
			tag = PAT
			tag = RIU
			tag = URG
			tag = CHL
			tag = ARG
			tag = NIC
			tag = HON
			tag = ELS
			tag = GUA
			tag = CUB
			tag = HAI
			tag = BWI
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
	}
	enable = {
		threat < 1
		has_war = no
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = global.country_in_south_america
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = USB
			}
			has_war = no
		}
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = ROOT.potential_and_current_enemies
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		all_of_scopes = {
			array = global.country_in_south_america
			is_ai = no
		}
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = global.start_americans
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = cavalry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = garrison			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = paratroopers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = mountaineers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = marines			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armor			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = light_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = heavy_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = medium_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = modern_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = infantry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armored_car		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = artillery		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = rocket			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized_rocket	value = -9999 }
}

ai_division_limiter_american_partical_stop = {
	allowed = {
		OR = {
			tag = JAM
			tag = COS
			tag = PAN
			tag = SUR
			tag = VEN
			tag = COL
			tag = ECU
			tag = KEC
			tag = PAR
			tag = PRU
			tag = PAU
			tag = JUL
			tag = PAT
			tag = RIU
			tag = URG
			tag = CHL
			tag = ARG
			tag = NIC
			tag = HON
			tag = ELS
			tag = GUA
			tag = CUB
			tag = HAI
			tag = BWI
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
	}
	enable = {
		threat > 0.99
		has_war = no
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = global.country_in_south_america
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = USB
			}
			has_war = no
		}
		NOT = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = ROOT.potential_and_current_enemies
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		all_of_scopes = {
			array = global.country_in_south_america
			is_ai = no
		}
		any_of_scopes = {
			array = global.start_americans
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = ARG
					original_tag = CHL
				}
			}
			num_divisions > 17
		}
		else = { num_divisions > 10 }
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = cavalry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = garrison			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = paratroopers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = mountaineers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = marines			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armor			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = light_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = heavy_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = medium_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = modern_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = infantry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armored_car		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = artillery		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = rocket			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized_rocket	value = -9999 }
}




#AI_DIVISION_LIMITER_TOTAL

ai_division_limiter_total = {
	allowed = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_total_limiter_status option = DEFAULT } }
	}
	enable = {
		NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_division_total_limiter_status option = DEFAULT } }
		check_variable = { global.total_division > global.total_division_limit }
		num_divisions > 0
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes

	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = cavalry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = garrison			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = paratroopers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = mountaineers		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = marines			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armor			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = light_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = heavy_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = medium_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = modern_armor		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = infantry			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = armored_car		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = artillery		value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = rocket			value = -9999 }
	ai_strategy = { type = build_army id = motorized_rocket	value = -9999 }
}



#AI_FORCE_BUILD_ARMIES_STATUS

ai_force_build_armies_up = {
	allowed = {
		has_game_rule = { rule = ai_force_build_armies_status option = AI_FORCE_BUILD_ARMIES_UP }
	}
	enable = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_force_build_armies_status option = AI_FORCE_BUILD_ARMIES_UP } has_manpower > 0 }
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	ai_strategy = { type = force_build_armies value = 1000 }
}
